preSubroutineBegin: s32'OnFrameStep'
ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal1)
  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(116000000)
  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(100001600)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(BattleDoing)
    ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
      ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
        ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
          callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'Magic_buff', Val(2), Val(1), Val(0), Val(0)
          if: Mem(ReturnValue)
            ifNot: Mem(EXBoss)
              sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 7, -32
            endIf: 
            else: 
              sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 7, -22
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei'
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'pot'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'pot', 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'fau'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(8)
      displayMesh: s32'Fau500cs', 1
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(9)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg7), Val(0)
      findState: s32'cmn_AfroObj', 11, 2, 52
      isObjectActive: (STACK7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK7)
          setObjectWidth: 1000
          setObjectHeight: 980
          setObjectDepth: 1000
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(10)
      isObjectActive: (STACK7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK7)
          setObjectWidth: 1000
          setObjectHeight: 970
          setObjectDepth: 1000
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(11)
      createObject: s32'ASK_fau500cs', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  if: Mem(BattleDoing)
    ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
      ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
        ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
          getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_ASK03', 2, 157
          if: Mem(TrainingValue)
            callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'Magic_buff', Val(1), Val(1), Val(0), Val(0)
            ifNot: Mem(ReturnValue)
              callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'Magic_buff', Val(1), Val(2), Val(0), Val(0)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_ASK04', 2, 157
          if: Mem(TrainingValue)
            callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'Magic_buff', Val(2), Val(1), Val(0), Val(0)
            ifNot: Mem(ReturnValue)

            if: Mem(ReturnValue)
              callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'Magic_buff', Val(2), Val(3), Val(0), Val(0)

    endIf:

beginSubroutine: s32'OnActionBegin'
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFWalk'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActBWalk'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFDash'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActBDash'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActAirFDash'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActAirBDash'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActJumpPre'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  upon: (SIGNAL_EX)
    if: Mem(SignalID)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_01', (SIGNAL1)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_02', (SIGNAL1)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_03', (SIGNAL1)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_05', (SIGNAL1)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_06', (SIGNAL1)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_10', (SIGNAL1)
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'Change_deck'
  ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
    checkInput: (INPUT_PRESS_P)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
      statsActionName: s32'Change_deck_A'
      createObject: s32'ChangeDeckCheckObj', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
    checkInput: (INPUT_PRESS_K)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(2)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
      statsActionName: s32'Change_deck_B'
      createObject: s32'ChangeDeckCheckObj', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
    checkInput: (INPUT_PRESS_S)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(3)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
      statsActionName: s32'Change_deck_C'
      createObject: s32'ChangeDeckCheckObj', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
    if: Mem(CPUVal0)
      ifOperation: (PERCENT), Val(50), Val(100)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(-1)
      endElse: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(4)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(3)
      endIf: 
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

          modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(ReturnValue), Val(10000)
          modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
        endIf: 
      endIf:

        modifyVar2: (MUL), Val(1), Val(10000)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(225)
        modifyVar2: (MUL), Val(2), Val(10000)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(226)
        modifyVar2: (MUL), Val(3), Val(10000)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(227)
        modifyVar2: (MUL), Val(4), Val(10000)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(228)
        modifyVar2: (MUL), Val(5), Val(10000)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(ExGauge4)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(200)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(24)
          modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(ReturnValue), Val(100000)
          modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(124)
          modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(ReturnValue), Val(100000)
          modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(224)
        modifyVar2: (MUL), Val(1), Val(100000)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(225)
        modifyVar2: (MUL), Val(2), Val(100000)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
      endIf:

        modifyVar2: (MUL), Val(3), Val(100000)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)

      endIf:

  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
    returnValue: 0, 1
    modifyVar2: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(100)
    modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(Tmp), Val(100)
    modifyVar2: (SUB), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(11)
      returnValue: 0, 2
      modifyVar2: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(100)
      modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(Tmp), Val(100)
      modifyVar2: (SUB), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)

      modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(Tmp), Val(100)
      modifyVar2: (SUB), Mem(ObjReg6), Mem(Tmp)
    endIf:

      returnValue: 0, 5

          storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(8)
        endIf:

    endElse:

  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(ActReg2)

beginSubroutine: s32'Magic_Func5'
  upon: (IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(3)
      callSubroutine: s32'Magic_PreEffFunc'
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(10)
      callPrivateFunction: s32'ClearPastSenkoInputTime', 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
      resetEasyInputP: 
      resetEasyInputK: 
      resetEasyInputS: 
      resetEasyInputHS: 
      bufferSpecialInput: 45
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(10)
      callSubroutine: s32'Magic_CheckInput'
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ReturnValue)
    endIf: 
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(-2), Mem(ActReg5)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(5)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(0), Mem(ActReg5)
    endIf:

      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(21)

beginSubroutine: s32'Draw_or_Discard'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
    ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
      sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 1, 420
    endIf: 
    else: 
      sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 1, 420
    endElse: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK1), 0, 1
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK1), 1, 1
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(2)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK2), 0, 1
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK2), 1, 1
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(3)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK3), 0, 1
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK3), 1, 1
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK1), 0, 2
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK1), 1, 2
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(2)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK2), 0, 2
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK2), 1, 2
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(3)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK3), 0, 2
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK3), 1, 2
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK1), 0, 3
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK1), 1, 3
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(2)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK2), 0, 3
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK2), 1, 3
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(3)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK3), 0, 3
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK3), 1, 3
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(4)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK1), 0, 4
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK1), 1, 4
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(2)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK2), 0, 4
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK2), 1, 4
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(3)
        ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
          sendSignalEx: (STACK3), 0, 4
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendSignalEx: (STACK3), 1, 4
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
    enableWhiffCancel: 1
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Magic_A'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Magic_A_air'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Magic_B'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Magic_B_air'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Magic_C'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Magic_C_air'

    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Magic_D_air'

    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Draw_or_Discard_A_air'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Draw_or_Discard_B'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Draw_or_Discard_B_air'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Draw_or_Discard_C'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Draw_or_Discard_C_air'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Draw_or_Discard_D'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'Draw_or_Discard_D_air'
